  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText12152430503844159154" style="display:none"><p>THIS IS A STORY ABOUT SACRIFICE... DEATH... LOVE... FREEDOM. THIS IS A STORY ABOUT FOREVER.</p> <p>Haven Antonelli and Carmine DeMarco grew up under vastly different circumstances. Haven, a second-generation slave, was isolated in the middle of the desert, her days full of hard work and terrifying abuse. Carmine, born into a wealthy Mafia family, lived a life of privilege and excess. Now, a twist of fate causes their worlds to collide. Entangled in a web of secrets and lies, they learn that while different on the surface, they have more in common than anyone would think. In a world full of chaos, where money and power rule, Haven and Carmine yearn to break free, but a string of events that began before either of them were born threatens to destroy them instead. </p> <p>Murder and betrayal are a way of life, and nothing comes without a price-especially not freedom. But how much will they have to sacrifice? Can they escape their pasts? And, most of all, what does it mean to be free?</p></span>

<div id="review_1270571288" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1270571288" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1270571288?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781465854889" href="/book/show/13664803-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=adventure-mystery-crime-thriller">adventure-mystery-crime-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1270571288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11063534923987678514">I absolutely loved this book. The title totally stunning…everything about this story is in some way summed up in that title!<br/><br/>It’s Godfather & Cinderella!!<br/>It’s thought-provoking.<br/>It’s about love.<br/>It’s about teenage angst.<br/>It’s about family love.<br/>It’s about loss.<br/>It’s about the challenges in life.<br/>It’s about human slavery, the mafia.<br/>It’s about loyalty.<br/>It’s about sacrifices.<br/>It’s about heartbreak<br/>It’s about murder.<br/><br/>Even after a week, I am still thinking about the story, the writing and the characters. <blockquote>
  
  </blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11063534923987678514" style="display:none">I absolutely loved this book. The title totally stunning…everything about this story is in some way summed up in that title!<br><br>It’s Godfather &amp; Cinderella!!<br>It’s thought-provoking.<br>It’s about love.<br>It’s about teenage angst.<br>It’s about family love.<br>It’s about loss.<br>It’s about the challenges in life.<br>It’s about human slavery, the mafia.<br>It’s about loyalty.<br>It’s about sacrifices.<br>It’s about heartbreak<br>It’s about murder.<br><br>Even after a week, I am still thinking about the story, the writing and the characters. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767024.png" alt=" photo download 3_zpsyecprbay.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> <br>This is really a love story between two teens, <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767025.png" alt=" photo download 1_zpsfhtbv6pc.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> from totally different backgrounds that are thrown together by, I guess, fate.<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430665419i/14743890.gif" alt=" photo b16ec04b-decf-4ce6-b991-9badb129457a_zpsrtyblhl5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">How they find love and healing despite the many obstacles in their way to finding happiness together. Their chemistry and emotional connection was really amazing…and so sweet.<br>Carmine never deviated from what he felt for Haven. He knew she was the person he had always been waiting for. <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767026.png" alt=" photo download 4_zpsgxnuyibb.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>The intensity of his feelings for Haven was deep and emotional….<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767027.jpg" alt=" photo large_zpsk2nuyzmd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>From a life of a human slave, never being loved, except for her mother, and never knowing anything about a life outside her cage, suddenly meets a human being who cares and loves her. <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767028.jpg" alt=" photo images201_zpswwfeml0s.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>Carmine made her believe, for the first time in her life, that just maybe there was something good out there for her and just adored how he supported her and gave her the confidence to do it. <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430665484i/14743919.jpg" alt=" photo beach-happiness-ocean-running-sunset-Favim.com-191893_zpsk5qzuxjm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>The characters are so human and believable and you are pulled into their lives and see the good and bad sides of them and the struggles they go through.<br>I was fascinated by Carmine’s father, Dr de Marco. Here is a man with so many secrets, such hidden feelings, who has done some pretty bad things but despite those things, I felt his pain as he tried to find redemption and do anything to protect his family that he loves so much.<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767029.gif" alt=" photo bd43625b-cc87-4d9b-8330-e58f0edf6559_zpswj8kabem.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>What I also enjoyed about this book is how I never knew where the story was going to. Who were the real good and bad guys? Would Carmine &amp; Haven find happiness together?<br><br>It’s a long book, full of details and characters but I was never bored. I just kept turning page after page…..you know the kind of book you never want it to end but you so want to know the ending? This is was one of those.<br><br>And the ending…..wow……..<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430832224i/14767030.png" alt=" photo download_zpsvjy18qag.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>I can’t wait to start the next installment.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11063534923987678514" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_293066727" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/293066727" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/293066727?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781456527730" href="/book/show/13111733-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer293066727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6546626382768804870"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384902252i/7023316._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>5 stars!!<br/><br/><b> "<i>Could someone do bad things, but not be a bad person? </i>" </b><br/><br/>I loved this book!! It was a beautiful, yet quietly powerful read.<br/><br/>It did a fantastic job of blurring the lines between good and bad. So many times when reading it I felt conflicted. Everything about some of the situations was so wrong but at the same time, I was liking, maybe even loving, the characters who were doing evil actions. Good guys put in bad situations, forced to make hard decisions that made them do wrong things for t</span>
  <span id="freeText6546626382768804870" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384902252i/7023316._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5 stars!!<br><br><b> "<i>Could someone do bad things, but not be a bad person? </i>" </b><br><br>I loved this book!! It was a beautiful, yet quietly powerful read.<br><br>It did a fantastic job of blurring the lines between good and bad. So many times when reading it I felt conflicted. Everything about some of the situations was so wrong but at the same time, I was liking, maybe even loving, the characters who were doing evil actions. Good guys put in bad situations, forced to make hard decisions that made them do wrong things for the right reasons but in the end the wrong thing to do actually ended up being the right thing... Yeah, if that confuses you, it sure as hell confused me too lol. And I loved it!!!<br><br>The story was quite the emotional roller coaster... I cried a little, I laughed a little, it made me care a lot for the characters.<br><br>The main character, Haven, is a second generation slave who grew up in a horribly abusive household and is bought into a Mafia family where she ends up falling in love with Carmine, the handsome, hot-headed yet inwardly tormented son of the man who bought her.<br><br><i>[Carmine] never went looking for it, but trouble seemed to find him every time he turned a corner. And Carmine turned a lot of motherfucking corners.</i><br><br>The book is long. 530 pages. But I didn't want to stop reading. At times it is a little slow, in the sense that its not always a burning page turner, but don't let that put you off. The story takes its time in the right places, it takes its time as Haven and Carmine fall in love, as she starts to recover from her abuse, and as she begins to come out of her shell. Sometimes I like books that don’t just rush through the story – it helps me immerse myself even more in the world and in the character’s lives.<br><br><i>“Colpo di fulmine. The thunderbolt, as Italians call it. When love strikes someone like lightning, so powerful and intense it can’t be denied. It’s beautiful and messy,cracking a chest open and spilling their soul out for the world to see. It turns a person inside out, and there’s no going back from it. Once the thunderbolt hits, your life is irrevocably changed.” </i><br><br>I love how this story explores boundaries and extremes. Master/slave, good/evil, right/wrong, excusable/justifiable actions... I'd say the over all theme though of the story is sacrifice.. Does the ends justify the means? To what ends are you willing to go for the ones you love?<br><br><b> <i>Right there in the moment, it was just her and him, no one and nothing else. They were all that mattered - two people, desperately in love and wanting to show each other. No master and slave, no class divides. </i> </b><br><br>And I fell in love with all the Italian endearments that Carmine calls Haven - they just melted my heart!!... I love Haven's quiet strength, and Carmine's fierce protectiveness of her. I loved that he was a character who could be an ass on minute but then have no problems apologizing and admitting it and trying to do better. It felt very honest. He made mistakes and tried again. <br><br><b> <i>There was an ache in his chest, originating in the center of his heart. It was the pain of all-consuming, overflowing love, so powerful it took his breath away. <br>"Do you feel this? We belong together." He kissed her. "<i> Sempre.</i>"</i> </b><br><br><i>“They're titles other people give us. They don't make us who we are. If you're just a slave, then I'm nothing more than a Principe. Is that all I am, Haven? A Mafia Prince?<br>"No, of course not."<br>That's what I thought," he said. "Just because some people see us that way doesn't mean it's what we are. We'll overcome our labels together. They don't matter, they don't make us who we are. We make us who are are. Fuck those motherfuckers."<br>She laughed. "When did you get so smart?"<br>"Baby, I've always been smart," he said playfully. "I'm just lazy as hell and rarely show it.” </i><br><br>I fell in love with the whole DeMarco family. Dominic, Carmine's brother, was delightful! Light hearted, caring and protective. And Vincent, the father... I'll admit he made me a little swoon-y at times. It was really great that the author took the time to tell his story and to get inside his head because it gave such insight to the 'why' behind so many questionable actions throughout the story. I'd love to read a book about him. The bits of the book about him and his wife made me teary. <br><br>This tension in this book comes from all unanswered questions. Who is Haven? How can she, a slave, and Carmine, the son of a high ranking Mafia member be together? Who is the good guy? Who is the bad guy? To what lengths will people go to save the one's they love?<br><br>The first 70% of the book is very character driven. And then all the pieces come together and everything kind of blows up and I almost felt like I was watching a movie, instead of reading a book for the last 30%... lots of action, lots of Mafia warring... quite delicious!<br><br>I loved watching Haven's inner and outer strength develop over the course of the book. I loved how fiercely she and Carmine loved each other, how he wouldn't let anyone look down on her... <br><br>This book had a happy ending but definitely left the story open for more development. <br><br><b> <i>“How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br>“I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br>“Why?”<br>“Because it doesn’t.” </i> </b><br><br>The author is writing a sequel now and I know I'll be buying it the day it comes out!!<br><br>I'd definitely recommend this book. I have nothing else to compare it to... but its definitely worth a read! *heading off to Amazon to buy a hard copy for my bookshelf*<br><br><b> ** EDIT ** OMG!! SEMPRE GOT A MOVIE DEAL!!!!! I'm so excited I can barely type this! *SQUEEEE* </b><br><br>Here's how I see Carmine and Haven:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380372158i/725367._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, come visit my book blog at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/">http://aestasbookblog.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6546626382768804870" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6179408006809261362"><b>5 stars!</b> <br/><br/>This book captivated me from the beginning. What a story! <i>Sempre</i> is a story about choices, sacrificing everything for the ones you love, intense true love, and then you throw in some human trafficking/slavery and mafia connections.<br/><br/>It was heartbreaking at times, but I loved the story and loved the characters (Carmine and Haven). It's one of those books that shows sometimes you are born into a certain life and many things are beyond your control, but sometimes two people who appear to com</span>
  <span id="freeText6179408006809261362" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!</b> <br /><br />This book captivated me from the beginning. What a story! <i>Sempre</i> is a story about choices, sacrificing everything for the ones you love, intense true love, and then you throw in some human trafficking/slavery and mafia connections.<br /><br />It was heartbreaking at times, but I loved the story and loved the characters (Carmine and Haven). It's one of those books that shows sometimes you are born into a certain life and many things are beyond your control, but sometimes two people who appear to come from totally different worlds can have more ties to each other than imaginable. <br /><br />I would recommend this book to everyone! Only have good things to say about it!</span>

<div id="review_1150928928" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1150928928" />
    <a title="Hulya Kara Yuksel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32793174-hulya-kara-yuksel"><img alt="Hulya Kara Yuksel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480666817p2/32793174.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1150928928?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hulya Kara Yuksel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hulya Kara Yuksel" href="/user/show/32793174-hulya-kara-yuksel">Hulya Kara Yuksel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18906167-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1150928928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6566418226889130003">Attention please! SEMPRE is going to be a movie!!! I don't have too much information about it yet but I'm going to share it with you as long as I get it. ❤<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.instagram.com/p/B21a5HLhKCI/?igshid=fax346mnemgc'>https://www.instagram.com/p/B21a5HLhK...</a><br/><br/>-------------------<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452695447ra/17728197.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Normally I don’t prefer to read long books. Long books give me pressure BUT this book.. My God, this story… I can read the damn book over and over again…. It was amazing. It was pure perfection! I loved it, I loved it so much! It was a really unforgeattable reading for me… :)<br/> <br/>Forget al</span>
  <span id="freeText6566418226889130003" style="display:none">Attention please! SEMPRE is going to be a movie!!! I don't have too much information about it yet but I'm going to share it with you as long as I get it. ❤<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/p/B21a5HLhKCI/?igshid=fax346mnemgc">https://www.instagram.com/p/B21a5HLhK...</a><br><br>-------------------<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452695447ra/17728197.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Normally I don’t prefer to read long books. Long books give me pressure BUT this book.. My God, this story… I can read the damn book over and over again…. It was amazing. It was pure perfection! I loved it, I loved it so much! It was a really unforgeattable reading for me… :)<br> <br>Forget all the mafia stories you read before and don’t expect too much action with every page but still there is a great story in this book and great mystery… But above all of that there is in love.. And of course there are a lot of other things going on around Carmine &amp; Haven. The tension of the story is simply amazing and it will give you thrill so much… I read the book in 3 days and when I finished the book my eyes were burning from too much reading but fuck it! I loved it a lot.... I enjoyed very much every damn minute. :) Especially when I read the last chapters of the book OMFG my hands were shaking… :) I loved how Carmine worship Haven. I loved how Haven gave her soul to Carmine. They’re perfect together… :)<br><br>And I won’t write to you the full story here but all you need is to know this book is about a boy and a girl… About their love, sacrifice and freedom. And their choices for themselves or for their beloved ones… And about How this two broken souls find each other by fate… I’m a hopeless romantic. I believe fate and I believe soul mate. Cause I’m married with my soul mate.. :) And when you read this book you’ll see how to love somebody and be loved in return can chance your life. And maybe because of that Carmine &amp; Haven’s story touched my heart so bad… <br><br><b>Ps. Can't wait to read 3rd book "MADE". I'm really excited Corrado &amp; Celia's story. :)</b><br><br><i>"When he touched her, she didn’t feel so alone. When he touched her, she felt alive for once..."<br><br>“Grabbing her hand, he pressed it gently to his chest. His skin was warm to the touch, and she could slightly feel his pulse pounding against her palm.<br>“Do you feel that? I’m not going anywhere, Haven. This is yours.” <br><br>“How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br>“I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br>“Why?”<br>“Because it doesn’t.”</i><br><br><b>Ps. If you wanna read this series, I suggest you to read with this order...<br>* Sempre<br>* Sempre:Redemption<br>* Friends - Novella<br>* Forever - Novella<br>* Made</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441584062ra/16125536.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400790414ra/9722142.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>--------------------------<br><br>“She hadn't known what love was, but she knew it now. Love was the fluttering in her tummy whenever Carmine was near, the twinkle in his eye when he laughed, the heat in her body from his words. Love was happy. Love was safe. Love was green. Love was him, the beautifully flawed boy who made her glow” <br><br>"Do you think you could ever love someone like me? She found the nerve to bring up a subject he wasn’t brave enough to broach, to utter the word love that terrified him so much, and instead of reassuring her he clammed up. <br>“Haven, I could never love someone like you, because there isn’t anyone else like you. You’re one of a kind.”<br><br>“My mom used to talk about fate all the time, and I think you’re it… you’re my fate. You were brought to me for a reason, for us to save each other. Because you weren’t the only one needing saved, Haven. I was drowning, and you rescued me.” <br><br>“How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br>“I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br>“Why?”<br>“Because it doesn’t.” <br><br>“Colpo di fulmine. The thunderbolt, as Italians call it. When love strikes someone like lightning, so powerful and intense it can’t be denied. It’s beautiful and messy,<br>cracking a chest open and spilling their soul out for the world to see. It turns a person inside out, and there’s no going back from it. Once the thunderbolt hits, your life is<br>irrevocably changed.” <br><br>"Do you have any idea how important you are to me?” he asked, pulling from her lips. “I’m finding myself again because of you. I never thought it would happen. My mom used to talk about fate, and I think you’re it . . . you’re my fate. You were brought to me for a reason, for us to save each other.” <br><br>“Grabbing her hand, he pressed it gently to his chest. His skin was warm to the touch, and she could slightly feel his pulse pounding against her palm.<br>“Do you feel that? I’m not going anywhere, Haven. This is yours.” <br><br>“See how much she’s changed… you did that for her”<br>“I didn’t do anything”<br>“You’re the one who made the difference … no matter what you do tomorrow, Carmine, what matters is that you did that today.”<br>“All I did was love her.”<br>“Ever think maybe that’s what she needed? Sometimes we don’t have to really do anything. We just have to be.” <br><br>“Tell me, Mr. DeMarco. What’s love to you?”<br>[…]<br>He glared at his teacher. “I think it’s ridiculous you’re even trying to define it like it’s something material you can just go find if you want it. People use the word too loosely as it is. They say they love this and they love that, when they don’t. They just like the shi— uh, stuff. Love is something that changes you, and if you really loved all the crap you say you love, you’d never know who you were because you’d constantly be changing. Once you love, you love forever. You can’t help it.” <br><br>“Sogni dóro, mia bella ragazza,” he mumbled, closing his eyes. "Sweet dreams my beautiful girl.” <br><br>""When he touched her, she didn’t feel so alone. When he touched her, she felt alive for once..."<br><br>"Every “I hate you” echoing from her chest was followed by an “I love you” from his lips. Every time she begged him to let go, he told her he would be there forever. His hold was strong, his arms familiar, but it did nothing to take away her pain."<br><br>“Some things in life only happen once, the memories of them lasting forever. They're moments that alter you, turning you into a person you never thought you'd become, but someone you were always destined to be. There's no magical rewind button in life, no take backs or do-over's to fix things you wish you could change.” <br><br>"Carmine,” she said. The sound of his name on her lips made his chest swell with love despite the fear. Nothing would ever overpower it. He stared into her deep brown eyes and it seemed as if time stopped. It always would, he realized. Carmine’s world wouldn’t go on without her.<br>“I love you, too,” he said, struggling to fight back the emotion so as not to scare her. “Sempre."<br><br>“You shouldn’t be afraid to take risks. It might not always work out, you might fail miserably and get hurt, but you’ll never know unless you try. And if it does work, wouldn’t it have been worth it?”</span>
  <a data-text-id="6566418226889130003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1089091945" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9311066705549642658">5 MILLION Tesoro Stars<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491073039i/22373834._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Grabbing her hand, he pressed it gently to his chest. His skin was warm to the touch, and she could slightly feel his pulse pounding against her palm.<br/>“Do you feel that? I’m not going anywhere, Haven. This is yours.”</i>
</b><br/> <br/>I mean, am I supposed to just go on after reading this thing?!<br/><br/>I know there are many reviews with the plot on here so I won't even go into it, but I just desperately needed to express my love for this story.<br/><br/>What perfect, emotional, heartbreaking, soul crushin</span>
  <span id="freeText9311066705549642658" style="display:none">5 MILLION Tesoro Stars<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491073039i/22373834._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Grabbing her hand, he pressed it gently to his chest. His skin was warm to the touch, and she could slightly feel his pulse pounding against her palm.<br>“Do you feel that? I’m not going anywhere, Haven. This is yours.”</i>
</b><br> <br>I mean, am I supposed to just go on after reading this thing?!<br><br>I know there are many reviews with the plot on here so I won't even go into it, but I just desperately needed to express my love for this story.<br><br>What perfect, emotional, heartbreaking, soul crushing, sweet, sad, incredible story. I literally had goose bumps the entire time, and was left with no fingernails after biting them all off from the suspense. This story is so insane and all the characters are so entwined I wouldn't even know where to start to go into details about the story line even if I wanted to. And what is most amazing about it is the simple way it's written. To me, it read so well each scene played out like a movie in my mind. If this was a movie, I would have watched it 7,356 times already.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I love you.” The words tumbled from her lips easily, like they had rolled from her tongue hundreds of times. But they hadn’t. She had never said them before, but as she heard them in her own voice, every cell in her body knew they were true. She hadn’t known what love was, but she knew it now. Love was the fluttering in her tummy whenever Carmine was near, the twinkle in his eyes when he laughed, the heat in her body from his words. Love was happy. Love was safe. Love was green. Love was him—the beautifully flawed boy who made her glow."</i>
</b><br><br>I will say this- Vincent- God at first I hated him and could not understand the man for the life of me. But as the story unfolded, I definitely understood and grew to love him. Especially at the end when he <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[finally accepts the past and accepts Haven and actually addresses her by her name. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> GODDDDDD SO SWEET. <br><br>Celia and Corrado are freaking amazing, Dominic is a sweet heart who I wished was my relative.<br><br>And the best for last – Carmine and Haven -SIGHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHH. I mean could a smart ass, impatient, foul-mouthed little rebel be any more amazing??! And Haven, oh sweet Haven. What an amazing, strong, sweet person she was. Their love was just epic. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I have a problem with my temper. It’s just, I feel . . .” He hesitated, taking a deep breath. “Look, it’s not because I think you belong to me—it’s because I want you to be mine.”</i>
</b><br><br>This is easily one of the <u>most incredible books I have ever read.</u> Definitely in my top favorites of all time. *UPDATE* MOST DEFINITELY MY MOST FAVORITE BOOK OF ALL TIME.<br><br>Now- I have wasted enough time writing this and wasted precious moments not reading Sempre: Redemption. I am off to meet with my sweet Carmine once again. I am so happy I was introduced to this story that made me fall in love and broke my heart all at the same time.<br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/552747526?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552747526" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9380586778206161942"><b>5+++ FOREVER STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412419454i/11373016.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Colpi di fulmine. The thunderbolt as Italians call it. When love strikes someone like lighting, so powerful and intense it can't be denied.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I've known about this book for a very long time, and everyone told me to read it. But for some reason I kept postponing it, until I just forgot about. But then I finally decided that I might as well read since the two books I've read by JM Darhower were both 4 or more stars. And I'm so glad I did! This is by far the best book by this </span>
  <span id="freeText9380586778206161942" style="display:none"><b>5+++ FOREVER STARS!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412419454i/11373016.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Colpi di fulmine. The thunderbolt as Italians call it. When love strikes someone like lighting, so powerful and intense it can't be denied.</i>
</b><br><br>I've known about this book for a very long time, and everyone told me to read it. But for some reason I kept postponing it, until I just forgot about. But then I finally decided that I might as well read since the two books I've read by JM Darhower were both 4 or more stars. And I'm so glad I did! This is by far the best book by this author... in my opinion. If you're looking for an epic love story, about love that overcomes the most trying obstacles and characters that will make you want to cry, hit something and basically feel intense emotions, well then, here you go!<br><br>Haven, was born into slavery, besides knowing that her mother loves her, it's the only other thing she's ever known. Her Master is a cruel man, she's never known kindness from anyone else but her mother. Until one day she decides to run, the same day she meets Dr DeMarco, the same day she starts her new life.<br><br>So for some reason this book almost destroyed my emotions, I'm not sure if it was because Haven was a just a young girl, who'd been so badly abused. Malnourished, beaten... Gah! I just can't! I mean it got me thinking! Somewhere in the world some girl is living the same life and there's no Dr DeMarco or sweet Carmine to save her. That's just how it is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412623417ra/11397992.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So how would you feel if you'd never known how freedom felt, and suddenly you were given just a small taste of how it would feel to be free. Haven's character was so strong, she's been added to my very short list of female characters I love! When Dr DeMarco, takes her to his home, her life becomes very different. This is one of those books where you'll love the characters one moment and hate them the next which is how I felt about Vincent and Carmine DeMarco. I loved them in the end but sometimes I felt like throat punching them because I felt like they were so insensitive to Haven's previous life. Especially Dr DeMarco, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I honestly started sobbing when he threatened to kill Haven by shoving a gun at her. She's just a child! I was inconsolable!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412619906i/11397417._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Carmine, started off being the arrogant and spoiled star athlete in the book. He had absolutely no regard for anyone but himself, he was promiscuous and didn't have much respect for women. That is until he sees Haven and gets to know her. Haven changed Carmine so much, her appreciation for the littlest things opened his eyes to the world. By the end of this book, Carmine knew about sacrifice and being prepared to lay down his life for the one he loves.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412619906i/11397418._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first half of this book was pretty good for me and I thought I was going to give it a solid fours stars. It started off very well, the combination of heart wrenching scenes and reading about Haven's struggles with acclimating herself to her new life and her budding relationship with Carmine kept me engaged. But the next half of the book was what finished the deal for me, mystery, action, romance and angst are some of the things I look for in a book and Sempre had that and so much more.<br><br>Mafia is all about La Famiglia and secrets are taken to the grave. When La Famiglia unravels, it's not a pretty thing. This book was fantastic! The perfect combination of dark, angst, romance and mafia all rolled up into an awesome Young Adult novel. If my recommendations mean anything to you, then you'll read this book!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9380586778206161942" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_324634247" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/324634247" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/324634247?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781465854889" href="/book/show/13664803-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer324634247" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7872263505135315272"><i>Sempre</i> is not your average feel-good love story. It is a gritty portrayal of various harsh realities and agonizing circumstances. Although my heart broke for the majority of this story, I enjoyed it immensely and found it both inspirational and humbling. I also found a new respect for individuals born into dreadful conditions beyond their control. <br/><br/><b>Haven</b> was born into slavery...and one could say that <b>Carmine</b> was born a slave to the pressures and expectations of following his father's footsteps in</span>
  <span id="freeText7872263505135315272" style="display:none"><i>Sempre</i> is not your average feel-good love story. It is a gritty portrayal of various harsh realities and agonizing circumstances. Although my heart broke for the majority of this story, I enjoyed it immensely and found it both inspirational and humbling. I also found a new respect for individuals born into dreadful conditions beyond their control. <br><br><b>Haven</b> was born into slavery...and one could say that <b>Carmine</b> was born a slave to the pressures and expectations of following his father's footsteps into the mafia. On the outside, Haven and Carmine have had vastly different childhoods—but upon closer inspection, their lives were all too similar. Their love for each other was young, but true and deep—and I enjoyed watching it blossom into maturity. Although this book was focused on very serious and sometimes dark subjects, there were also many moments of fun and lightheartedness, for which I was grateful. <br><br>This beautiful story is as intense as it is touching. It's about <b>redemption</b> and<b> hope</b>.  Its about sacrificing everything in the name of love no matter what the cost. It's about dying for what you believe in, but ultimately, it's about being able to just truly<b> LIVE</b>.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Mild/sexy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Complex, intense, and beautiful young love. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Protective hero. Heartbreakingly damaged and abused heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> An intense, unconventional love story focused on pain, redemption, and hope. (*Human trafficking*)<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Passionate. Poetic. Gorgeous. Compelling. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 3rd Person Perspective<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> Mild/doable. Ending open for more story. <br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Follow up.<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <a title="Debra Anastasia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4619038-debra-anastasia"><img alt="Debra Anastasia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593759570p2/4619038.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271331753?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra Anastasia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra Anastasia" href="/user/show/4619038-debra-anastasia">Debra Anastasia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781456527730" href="/book/show/13111733-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271331753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13135471346334197625">Sempre was fantastic. It is a real reader's book. Knowing this book was self published explains a lot. It is a raw story, straight from the author's imagination and heart. It shows. Sempre was a treat for me, after I had completed the day's tasks, I'd get to read until my eyes gave up. Carmine and Haven became alive. You want everything good for them. There is action, romance, and a great plot. There's also a much bigger purpose for the book. It shines an unflinching spotlight on modern day slav</span>
  <span id="freeText13135471346334197625" style="display:none">Sempre was fantastic. It is a real reader's book. Knowing this book was self published explains a lot. It is a raw story, straight from the author's imagination and heart. It shows. Sempre was a treat for me, after I had completed the day's tasks, I'd get to read until my eyes gave up. Carmine and Haven became alive. You want everything good for them. There is action, romance, and a great plot. There's also a much bigger purpose for the book. It shines an unflinching spotlight on modern day slavery. <br /><br />Darhower does one of my very favorite things--blurring the lines between the good guys and the shining white knights. She does it so effortlessly, I actually smiled when I realized I was heartbroken because a murderer was injured. That takes some serious talent. <br /><br />I hope you decide to treat yourself to this book. Please remember that it's not chick lit. This isn't bubblegum, gigglepants stuff, though you will laugh at times. It's novel with a journey that feels very important to take. Load it up on your eReader, you will not be disappointed. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13135471346334197625" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2148816770" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2148816770" />
    <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell"><img alt="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584062476p2/2190064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2148816770?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell">Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=halloween-2017-reading-challenge">halloween-2017-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kindle-freebie-graveyard">kindle-freebie-graveyard</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=urr-botms">urr-botms</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2148816770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2448003108279012559"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>🎃 Read for the Unapologetic Romance Readers <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/18923237-halloween-2017-reading-challenge' rel='nofollow noopener'>Halloween 2017 Reading Challenge</a>
</b> for the category of: <i>a romance novel with blood on the cover</i> 🎃<br/><br/><br/><br/>Good books make you ask questions - but sometimes, bad books make you ask questions, too. Questions like, "Why is this book so <i>long</i>?" "How did this even get published?" And, most pressingly, "What is it about this book that people actually <i>like</i>?"<br/><br/><br/><br/>I read SEMPRE for our book of the month over at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/187063-unapologetic-romance-readers' rel='nofollow noopener'>URR</a>,</span>
  <span id="freeText2448003108279012559" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>🎃 Read for the Unapologetic Romance Readers <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/18923237-halloween-2017-reading-challenge" rel="nofollow noopener">Halloween 2017 Reading Challenge</a>
</b> for the category of: <i>a romance novel with blood on the cover</i> 🎃<br><br><br><br>Good books make you ask questions - but sometimes, bad books make you ask questions, too. Questions like, "Why is this book so <i>long</i>?" "How did this even get published?" And, most pressingly, "What is it about this book that people actually <i>like</i>?"<br><br><br><br>I read SEMPRE for our book of the month over at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/187063-unapologetic-romance-readers" rel="nofollow noopener">URR</a>, and am only just now finishing it because of how awful it was. It wasn't even spectacularly awful - just dismally so. Everything about this book <i>dragged</i>. Most of those 500 pages? They're all padding. The story, without all that fluff, is pretty simple. Haven is a teenage <i>slave</i>. Carmine's father <i>buys </i>her. He falls in love with his slave, and she falls in love with him, and it's all hearts and cuddles and tender moments - until the mafia steps in and says, "Hell <i>no</i>."<br><br><br><br>I hate to say it, but I was on the mafia's side in this one. I was like, "Hell <i>no</i>," too.  <br><br><br><br>Here's my biggest issue. SEMPRE reads like the author wanted to write fanfic of Goodfellas, Godfather, and Sopranos, but she also <i>really </i>wanted to write a disgustingly fluffy book like Stephanie Perkins, but she <i>also </i>wanted to write a really edgy new adult book with SEX, but she <i>also </i>really wanted her hero to be a Nice Guy, but she <i>also </i>really wanted her heroine to be pure and virtuous.<br><br><br><br>Even though, you know, she grew up in a world of sex trafficking. <br><br><br><br>So what we have is a PG-13 mafia/human trafficking book where most of the book takes place in high school and there's a few random scenes that seem to be heavily inspired by the three mafia books I mentioned, all written from Carmine's father's POV. Haven is a slave, whose mother is basically a sex slave, but Haven herself is used for cooking and cleaning and that's it. She's innocent about everything, and even asks, in all seriousness, whether there are colleges in California.<br><br><br><br>WHAT.<br><br><br><br>I mean, there's sheltered, and then there's how-the-hell-did-you-not-know-that.<br><br><br><br>Carmine is everything I hate in a hero. He swears a lot and punches people out to show how tough he is, and Darhower desperately tries to make him the good guy by punching out these people on Haven's behalf and having all these forced intimate moments with her. Forced in the technical sense, that is: not the rapey sense. And Haven is so naive that she makes me sick. You can tell that she's just supposed to be so <i>adorable </i>because she nibbles at food, nuzzles at people, peers up at people, and chases fireflies while the adoring Carmine just sits there and smiles in vacant admiration because that's what people do when they watch cat videos, and Haven is basically supposed to be the human equivalent of a cat video - only for some reason, it's not cute when a person does it, just disturbing.<br><br><br><br>I'm still blown away by how boring and terrible this was, and that it has a 4.2 average rating on Goodreads (did we read different books?). SEMPRE took a dar topic and tried to make it a cute love story. The result is a book that comes across as both tone deaf and ridiculous.<br><br><br><br>1 star</span>
  <a data-text-id="2448003108279012559" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_283537790" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/283537790" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/283537790?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781465854889" href="/book/show/13664803-sempre">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Karla by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=angst-filled">angst-filled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=pain">pain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=sweet-romance">sweet-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=tortured-souls">tortured-souls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=violence">violence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=intense">intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=family-drama">family-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=passionate">passionate</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer283537790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16648771554372500406"><b>4.5 Stars Riveting!</b><br/>I had a love/hate relationship with this book, this story, and these characters. What I mean is that the life they live and the things they do, I would never condone, but in their world, the mafia <i>famiglia</i>, it is the norm and the story is based on that. I constantly questioned their actions, but as the story unfolds you come to understand, and past history, why they react so severely to certain situations and need to have total control. <br/><br/>Haven is the teenage slave that Dr. Vinc</span>
  <span id="freeText16648771554372500406" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars Riveting!</b><br />I had a love/hate relationship with this book, this story, and these characters. What I mean is that the life they live and the things they do, I would never condone, but in their world, the mafia <i>famiglia</i>, it is the norm and the story is based on that. I constantly questioned their actions, but as the story unfolds you come to understand, and past history, why they react so severely to certain situations and need to have total control. <br /><br />Haven is the teenage slave that Dr. Vincent DeMarco “rescues” and I use that term loosely, because although her surroundings have improved, his hate for her is quite evident. I was not taken with Vincent, I found him to be lacking as a father, and his total disregard for Haven really put me out, but as the story progresses my heart feels for him and all that he has endured. He has two sons Dominic and Carmine, they live with him far from the world that all too often calls him back to Chicago. Dominic is sweet, easy going and embraces Haven as part of the family. Carmine is a hot-head, reckless and his abrasive personality has Haven running in the opposite direction. As they spend more time together she learns to relax around him and he becomes nurturing and protective of her. He’s still reckless, but is trying hard to be a better person for Haven. Theirs is a unique and unconventional love story. They are so young, and Vincent seems to look the other way when it comes to their close proximity, particularly their sleeping arrangements. Although for the most part of the book it is innocent, as much as it can be for two teens, it then progresses in sexual nature. I don’t know too many parents that would allow this, but again, this is not the “All American” family. You feel that Carmine and Haven are meant to be together, and the love they have for each other is undeniable. <br /><br />Then we meet Corrado, Vincent’s brother-in-law and Celia, Vincent's sister, mafia wife. I loved them. Corrado pulled the trigger without blinking an eye, human life disposable to him, but if it protected the <i>famiglia</i> he saw it as nothing more than necessary measure…and again I will reiterate that I loved him. Celia is all too aware of what her family is and what they do, but her love for her husband, brother and nephews, even Haven, is so evident that I could not help but love her. <br /><br />Halfway thru the books, the unveiling begins and that’s when I had trouble keeping up, because when you think you knew the answer or predict the outcome…no, no, no…it was not to be. I would get to the end of a chapter, tell myself to walk away, do something else, but I couldn’t. I was in it for the long haul. Talk about emotional overload…<b>EXHAUSTING!!</b> I hated the things that these people did, but yet I was rooting for them. Why?! The writing. You have now connected to these characters and you overlook the bad, and hope for the good…what is good for them! There is violence, there is death, and I cried. I never saw it coming, and it was like someone ripped my heart out of my chest. My predictions were for the most part unfounded and the author would then pull me in another direction, and again I assumed, and again I was wrong. <br /><br />These characters, this story, stayed with me, disrupted my life, had me lost in thought for hours, and I loved it. I did take issue with a few things, one being Haven’s swift recovery. She adjusted rather quickly and for someone who was sheltered from society, she seemed to be more knowledgeable than I would have expected. The other was the ending, way too abrupt and too much left to the imagination. I wanted closure, I needed closure, I wanted the end to be wrapped up with a pretty little bow. I didn’t get that. I hung in there for the whole book, a long book, when through the emotional wringer and I felt cheated, and those are my reasons for removing a half a star. <br /><br />Thank you Kristen for recommending this phenomenal read, it was everything you said it was! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16648771554372500406" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1570053096540476191">OMG. I love this book. I can't even describe how much I liked it. Maybe I'll review it later, now I'm feeling really emotional because it's over. Definetly worth reading.<br/><br/>LATER:<br/><br/>This book was simply amazing, it's a MUST-read. I loved everything about it. It has great character development and a good plot (with some really unexpected twists). Carmine DeMarco is hilarious (and really lovely) and OMG, I think I'm in love with Corrado Moretti, haven't met a more badass character than him! <br/><br/>All in all, </span>
  <span id="freeText1570053096540476191" style="display:none">OMG. I love this book. I can't even describe how much I liked it. Maybe I'll review it later, now I'm feeling really emotional because it's over. Definetly worth reading.<br /><br />LATER:<br /><br />This book was simply amazing, it's a MUST-read. I loved everything about it. It has great character development and a good plot (with some really unexpected twists). Carmine DeMarco is hilarious (and really lovely) and OMG, I think I'm in love with Corrado Moretti, haven't met a more badass character than him! <br /><br />All in all, this book deserves ALL THE STARS &lt;3. The love story is beautiful and not only that, this book has EVERYTHING, if you are looking for drama, suspense, action, humor and a good dosis of romance, you must read this. </span>

<div id="review_1073735783" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1073735783" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1073735783?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18906167-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-recs">buddy-recs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=smartass-witty-banters">smartass-witty-banters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=forbidden-taboo-love">forbidden-taboo-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=swoon-worthy-guys">swoon-worthy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=fluffy-fluffer">fluffy-fluffer</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=oh-look-pretty-cover">oh-look-pretty-cover</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1073735783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2986262200103307013"><b>5++ PER SEMPRE STARS! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414168162i/11617622.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Colpo di fulmine. The thunderbolt, as Italians call it. When love strikes someone like lightning, so powerful and intense it can’t be denied.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Ever know what it feels like to have your heart ripped out, stomped over and being handed back over to you <i>and then</i> to have it crushed yet again? Well, no? Really?<br/><br/><b>Read this one for ye almighty love that is this glorious book.</b><br/><br/><i><u>WARNING</u>: Possibly lengthy review ahead because that's how I deal with my feels when a book decides to</i></span>
  <span id="freeText2986262200103307013" style="display:none"><b>5++ PER SEMPRE STARS! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414168162i/11617622.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Colpo di fulmine. The thunderbolt, as Italians call it. When love strikes someone like lightning, so powerful and intense it can’t be denied.”</i>
</b><br><br>Ever know what it feels like to have your heart ripped out, stomped over and being handed back over to you <i>and then</i> to have it crushed yet again? Well, no? Really?<br><br><b>Read this one for ye almighty love that is this glorious book.</b><br><br><i><u>WARNING</u>: Possibly lengthy review ahead because that's how I deal with my feels when a book decides to rip my soul apart and owns my life. Don't say I didn't warn ya.</i><br><br>******* <br><br><b>Sempre</b> begins off with a fuzzy prologue which introduces <b>Haven Antonelli</b>, a modern slave that has been living off in a desert and is later being taken away by a man named <b>Vincent DeMarco</b>. Whisked off by this unknown man into his own home, Haven struggles to adjust with her new life as opposed to her old one where she has been abused; physically and mentally. <br><br>Living under this same roof is <b>Dominic &amp; Carmine DeMarco</b>, sons of Vincent; but only one of them will be hit by a whirlwind that is Haven. <br><br>In a story where family doesn't just equate to real bloodlines, loyalties will be tested and sacrifices will be made in this thrilling Mafia read as we embark into the lives of 'la famiglia'.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406283ra/792497.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>******* <br><br>Let me just say that I found it extremely hard to believe that this is the same author who wrote <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_" title="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Monster in His Eyes</a> because <b>Sempre evoked almost all humanly possible emotions in me</b> whereas MiHE did the total opposite. And this is also where I say, THANK HEAVENS that I decided to give this author another shot because <b>this book simply stripped me raw of my emotions and left me naked and crying in my puddle of feels.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414170996ra/11617906.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><s>Fuck, thinking of this book right now is already making me quiver.</s><br><br>I mean, <b>
  <i>fan-fucking-static book</i>
</b>. Honestly, I couldn't even tell that this book is mighty lengthy. One minute I plopped onto my bed and read it, next thing I know 2 hours had passed and I'm silently whimpering as I'm torn apart reading this epic beautiful love story that is Carmine and Haven. And the next morning I woke up late for work, go figure. #sorrynotsorry #ihavenoregrets<br><br><b>Haven</b>. I love that girl so <i>so</i> much. Her character is just all sorts of inspiring for me. <b>Her naivety and innocence at first had already captured my heart but it was her optimism that totally sold me.</b> Even after all the shit she's been through (which breaks my fucking heart), she was still such a brave soul and so eager to live. Even the foul-mouthed teenage boy saw something so alive flicker in her as he watched her in their library.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"“But then she happened. The girl who had never been able to call her life her own taught a boy who had the world at his fingertips exactly what it meant to live. He wasn’t alone anymore.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Also, that fireflies scene ♥♥♥ <b>IT FELT MAGICAL TO ME.</b> THERE I SAID IT. GO AHEAD AND JUDGE ME.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414170996ra/11617907.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And there's <b>Carmine</b>. He was a man-whore with a temper that flares and has a foul mouth that could fill up a potty mouth jar within a day or two. But with a past and a possible future that weighs down heavily on him, he was just another lost young soul. When he's with Haven, he realizes that a privileged boy like him is no different than this abused girl he's in love with; <b>both equally broken but still have the heart in them to help each other heal and live and love again.</b> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“How about we just be Haven and Carmine? We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br>“I like that. Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br>“Why?”<br><b>“Because it doesn’t."</b></i>
</blockquote> <br>This was the best kind of young love I could actually ask for. <b>Slow build-up but undeniable chemistry throughout.</b> The kind of bond that these two shared, the commitment they had for each other despite their contrasting background; <b>it was tough, raw, gritty, powerful</b>; jeezus it just sent my heart into a turmoil as I watched this couple reached every milestone in their relationship and all I can say is: <b>it was so heartachingly beautiful on so many levels.</b> FLUTTERS AND FEELS AND HEARTACHES.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Love was the fluttering in her tummy whenever Carmine was near, the twinkle in his eyes when he laughed, the heat in her body from his words. Love was happy. Love was safe. Love was green.<br><br><b>Love was him - the beautifully flawed boy who made her glow."</b></i>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406283ra/792504.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"And I love you. Per sempre."<br>"Sempre?"<br><b>"Always and forever."</b></i>
</blockquote><br>The entire Mafia aspect in this story also sucked me in so deep in this read. <b>I found myself perplexed with this entire "la famiglia" and the mystery surrounding it all made this book even more compelling than it already is.</b> Even the secondary characters are so well-developed! Thrilling, suspenseful and a whole lot of BAMF action from Vincent and Corrado (yes ladies, we're gonna to have a fight over this gentleman here), this book can only keep getting better from here on out. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Leave. Because I'll be forced to kill you if you don't, and I'm wearing my favorite shirt. It'll ruin my night to get your filthy blood on it." - Corrado</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410269744ra/11083799.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>**********<br><br>Well if you've made it through my feels, THANK YOU FOR LISTENING! ♥♥ If not, THANK YOU STILL! ♥♥ <b>If you've yet to read this book, READ IT.</b> I swear I won't put a gun to your head but read it if you you're looking for that one powerful motha of all love reads that has mafia written all over it. <br><br>All I can say is that <i>Sempre</i> is no doubt a story of <b>freedom, love, redemption, hope and sacrifice.</b> Ultimately, it shows you the depths of how far one is willing to go in the name of love. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"<b>Sempre.</b> No matter what happened next, or what went on tomorrow, nothing would ever take that away. Their love existed, depsite everything else, and it was that love that would go on forever. The moment was etched in time, transcending the constraints put on them by life."</i>
</blockquote> </span>
  <a data-text-id="2986262200103307013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
