<span id="freeTextContainer15515021713936219025"> <b>4,5 BEAUTIFUL STARS <33</b><br/><br/>This book is a true emotional roller coaster!!I fell in love with this book from the beginning wow it is really so good!!!I had so many emotions while I was reading it.. <br/>Both main characters go through so many bad things, but they still manage to get past all of them and start over....<br/><br/>This is about hope,faith,love and sacrifice..<br/><br/>Haven is a young, innocent girl who paid for the mistakes of others. ..She was born a slave..and she has been held captive...Until DeMarco who is</span>
  <span id="freeText15515021713936219025" style="display:none"> <b>4,5 BEAUTIFUL STARS &lt;33</b><br><br>This book is a true emotional roller coaster!!I fell in love with this book from the beginning wow it is really so good!!!I had so many emotions while I was reading it.. <br>Both main characters go through so many bad things, but they still manage to get past all of them and start over....<br><br>This is about hope,faith,love and sacrifice..<br><br>Haven is a young, innocent girl who paid for the mistakes of others. ..She was born a slave..and she has been held captive...Until DeMarco who is a part of mafia take her to live with him and his two sons Carmine and Dominic...<br><br>Carmine and Haven fall instantly in love...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384734944i/6947784.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how these two find each other..Their relationship wasn't easy and was forced with obstacle.It's not easy when you are in a family Mafia..They were forced to make decisions and sacrifices to save one another.. <br><br>But real love makes every sacrifices worth it...<br><br><br><b>"Do you have any idea how important you are to me?"<br>" I'm finding myself again because of you.I never thought it would happen.My mom used to talk about fate all the time and I think you're it...you're my fate.<br><br>"Ti amo tantissimo, mia bella ragazza."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384642461i/6923206.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Haven is really a remarkable character.She is innocent and vulnerable but even with all those awful things she experienced in her life she remained to be a very strong and intelligent character!!<br><br>Carmine...OMG *sigh* I love him!!!<br>He was a jerk at the beginning but when he meets Haven everything changes!!He started sees things different...<br>He loves her with a passion I've never seen before. There's absolutely nothing he wouldn't do for her.<br><br>If you haven't read it,you must read it right now!!<br>I'm sure that when you start it you will not able to put it down!!</span>

<div id="review_610886848" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610886848" />
    <a title="Kristalia " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia"><img alt="Kristalia " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1535637983p2/5705623.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610886848?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristalia " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristalia " href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia">Kristalia </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781456527730" href="/book/show/13111733-sempre">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristalia  by: </span>
      Naomi Soraya
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=age-new-adult">age-new-adult</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610886848" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1815456340189161740"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br/>“I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br/>“Why?”<br/>“Because it doesn’t.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br/><br/>✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ ✄ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ ☁ ☂ ✎ ✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ ✄ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ ☁ ☂ ✎ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Ti amo, mia bella ragazza. Per sempre.”<br/>“Sempre?” she asked.<br/>Cracking a smile, he brushed his pointer finger softly across her lips. “Always and forever.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br/><br/>✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ </span>
  <span id="freeText1815456340189161740" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br>“I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br>“Why?”<br>“Because it doesn’t.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ ✄ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ ☁ ☂ ✎ ✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ ✄ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ ☁ ☂ ✎ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Ti amo, mia bella ragazza. Per sempre.”<br>“Sempre?” she asked.<br>Cracking a smile, he brushed his pointer finger softly across her lips. “Always and forever.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ ✄ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ ☁ ☂ ✎ ✍ ☘ ❦ ☕ ❂ ✄ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ ☁ ☂ ✎ ☸ ⚡ ⚓ <br><br><b>WOW. FANTASTIC, FABULOUS, CAPTIVATING, ICOULDNTSTOPREADING TYPE OF A STORY!!!!</b> I am serious, whole time i was like... <br><br><br><blockquote>
<b>MY INNER SELF: </b> Stop reading now! You have your final exam tomorrow!<br><b>ME: </b> But i can't! I don't wanna stop!<br><b>MY INNER SELF: </b> But you must, you will fail!<br><b>ME: </b> I won't fail, even though i have no idea what i just read in the whole freaking exam book.<br><b>MY INNER SELF: </b> Then what are you waiting for?<br><b>ME: </b> Fine. *goes to study*<br><i> 20 minutes later... </i><br><b>SEMPRE: </b> read meeeeeeee...read meeeee...you wanna know what happens next!!!!!!! Look, in your exam book, look what i found:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420919i/835595.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>ME: </b><br>WTF!!!!!!!!!!<br>*falls out of trans* Please, stop, i am trying to learn....<br><i> 3 hours later... </i><br><b>MY INNER SELF: </b> ok, you can read now.<br><b>ME: </b> HELL YEAH!!!!<br><b>MY INNER SELF: </b> for 20 minutes....<br><b>ME: </b> I hate myself...<br><i> the next day </i><br><b>ME: </b> SEE I PASSED THE EXAM WITH 9 OF 10, CAN I FINISH THE BOOK NOW.<br><b>MY INNER SELF: </b> HELL YEAH.<br><b>ME: </b> vaffanculo, my inner self :(<br><b> THE END </b><br> </blockquote><br><br><b> Anyway, now that i finished retelling my imaginary conversation with myself, lemme tell you what i think of this book...</b> <br><br>I<b> loved it </b> - and<b> its the type of the book i would reread again and again</b> (which i kind of did when i finished the book.. i started from the beginning). <br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Some things in life only happen once, the memories of them lasting forever. they're moments that alter you, turning you into a person you never thought you'd become, but someone you were always destined to be.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>This story is not entirely pretty - insert mafia, family business and slavery and you know what to expect. But it's also a story of freedom and choices, of love and rivalry, of two broken teenagers... <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"They were two broken kids, desperate to be whole again, struggling to find balance in a world out of their control. What's black and white and red all over? Carmine was, Haven thought. A soul savagely ripped in half, bleeding out for all to see. The ying and yang, the good and evil, the love and pain all at odds with each other. Two sides, two vastly different worlds, but someday they’d merge as one. They had to."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>They try to understand each other... Haven and Carmine are born in different worlds, but they are the same inside... She was raised as a modern slave, he was raised as a mafia prince... But they are more alike then they thought they were...<br><br>But, this is not only a love story - danger is around the corner... And there is no escape.<br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Haven</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420919i/835599.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He smiled. She didn’t mind his company. “Do you wanna talk about what happened?”<br>“There’s nothing to talk about. I survived. That’s what I do. I’ll keep surviving until I don’t survive anymore.”<br>“So, you're saying you're a survivor?”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>Born as a slave, and raised as one, she knows the truth - She will never be free. Being abused, beaten and when finally threatened to be killed - she tries to escape...where she utterly fails. But, when Dr. Vincent DeMarco, who visited her 'master' takes her away, she finds out that there is more to life than she ever thought... <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Do we need to be saved?”<br>“Don't we always?” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>Haven is scared and afraid of the new life she is given... She tries to understand where she fits in the 'family' that now she belongs to. Haven thinks that she just changed masters and nothing else. She expects nothing, but is given more than she could hope for. Carmine. Dr. DeMarco's trouble maker son, the one who understands her more than anyone else.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “My mom used to talk about fate all the time, and I think you’re it… you’re my fate. You were brought to me for a reason, for us to save each other. Because you weren’t the only one needing saved, Haven. I was drowning, and you rescued me.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>I understood Haven... it's not easy when your life changes drastically and when your whole life is controlled by other people. So i found her reactions and feelings quite reasonable... I loved her, she tried her best, even when it was hard to cope with. <br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Carmine</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420919i/835600._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “But then she happened. The girl who had never been able to call her life her own taught a boy who had the world at his fingertips exactly what it meant to live. He wasn’t alone anymore.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>Carmine... broken inside... hell of a teenager outside... Trouble maker, womanizer, quite rude, reckless, likes to get in fights and everything else that follows the reputation of "bad boy".<br><br>But, Heaven changes him, as much as he changes her. She balances him out perfectly, and he dropped his every act, every anger he had toward world just to be the man he thought she would want him to be...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><br>“Tell me, Mr. DeMarco. What’s love to you?”<br>[…]<br>He glared at his teacher. “I think it’s ridiculous you’re even trying to define it like it’s something material you can just go find if you want it. People use the word too loosely as it is. They say they love this and they love that, when they don’t. They just like the shi— uh, stuff. Love is something that changes you, and if you really loved all the crap you say you love, you’d never know who you were because you’d constantly be changing. Once you love, you love forever. You can’t help it.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>i must say, i loved him quite a lot (because he never <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ cheated on her  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>) and i love him because even though he was trouble and walking disaster, he was still a good man on the inside. He just need someone to understand him.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Other characters</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br>They were fabulous. Deep, and well characterized. I love Vincent, Celia and Corrado,Nicholas, Dominic and even Maura and Haven's mother...they were fantastic characters. <br><br>Especially Vincent...i underestimated him in the beginning, i thought of him as evil SOB but he was someone else entirely. I loved him in the end.<br><br>And Corrado and Celia were great as well. I was impressed and shocked of what Corrado did near the end, to protect his own... <br><br>And Nicholas... he was understimated too...by me and by everyone else. And his jokes were really funny :D<br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>I highly recommend it... It's funny, heartbreaking, lovely, beautiful and just awesome. It's a story i wont forget for a long time ;)<br>Why are you still here? go read it :D</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Sogni dóro, mia bella ragazza,” he mumbled, closing his eyes. "Sweet dreams my beautiful girl.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><b> EDIT: </b><br><br>Awesome news :D Sempre was bought by Simon &amp; Schuster which means that it will be re-released November 4th as an ebook. With new stuff in it ♥<br>Now i can reread it again and with new experience (probably) :D <br>But if you have not read Sempre yet, better wait for re-release ;D<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> Sempre will be re-released November 4th as an ebook with revamped content. ACK! Don't worry, those who already own it... we've worked hard to make sure the plot isn't affected by the srs bsns editing we're undertaking on that bad boy, so your copy is just fine *pets self-published copy*. It'll just be more tightened and focused when it's re-released (and may or may not have some extended content of the sexual nature... but yeah... MOVING ON... DON'T KILL ME... I LOVE YOU).</i>
</blockquote> <br>-Taken from <a href="http://myblog.jmdarhower.com/2013/05/sempre-news.html" rel="nofollow noopener">JM Darhower’s blog post </a>♥<br><br>Can't wait ♥<br><br><br><b>
  <i>This review can be found on my blog: <a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">infinity-of-time.blogspot.com</a> also known as... </i>
</b><br><a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/2013/05/sempre-forever-1-by-jm-darhower.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380363317i/714576.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476734194" href="/book/show/17571164-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=5-stars-read">5-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer569990852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12095312040634753896"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142151.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Million stars! A must-read and definitely my all time favourite.<br/><u>NOW AGAIN LIVE ON <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Sempre-J-M-Darhower-ebook/dp/B00BSBVFWC/ref=tmm_kin_swatch_0?_encoding=UTF8&sr=&qid=' rel='nofollow noopener'>AMAZON</a>!</u><br/><br/>My Haven and Carmine:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142152._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i><b>Carmine DeMarco</b> is troubled, tempramental and problematic teenage boy who does what he wants and when he wants. He doesn't really care about anything until Haven comes along...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142153._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i><b>Haven Antonelli</b> knows nothing else as being unequal, a slave, a servant. When she is put with DeMarco family, the life she knew so far is turned upside down. Will she be able to adapt?</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142154._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Italian mafia, slavery, freedo</span>
  <span id="freeText12095312040634753896" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142151.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Million stars! A must-read and definitely my all time favourite.<br><u>NOW AGAIN LIVE ON <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Sempre-J-M-Darhower-ebook/dp/B00BSBVFWC/ref=tmm_kin_swatch_0?_encoding=UTF8&amp;sr=&amp;qid=" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a>!</u><br><br>My Haven and Carmine:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142152._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><b>Carmine DeMarco</b> is troubled, tempramental and problematic teenage boy who does what he wants and when he wants. He doesn't really care about anything until Haven comes along...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142153._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><b>Haven Antonelli</b> knows nothing else as being unequal, a slave, a servant. When she is put with DeMarco family, the life she knew so far is turned upside down. Will she be able to adapt?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142154._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Italian mafia, slavery, freedom, danger, love and sacrifice. All these are topics of this book. This story reminded me to never take anything for granted and to enjoy simple things every day. <br><br>Sempre is extremely <b>powerful</b> and intese story. The one that you will never forget. It was beautiful and fascinating to read about two poeple from completely different backgorunds growing close together and falling in love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385404993i/7142155.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Amazingly crafted characters, excellent writing, captivating storyline. This story was <b>flawless</b>! The use of 3rd person narrative made it very special for me. As a reader, I was able to connect with main as well as supporting characters and all of them became very close to my heart.<br><br>I can't express how much I love this story. Mrs. Darhower put her soul into it and I savoured every single word she wrote. As soon as you can, I highly recommend you to pick this book up and read it. You won't regret it.<br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a><br><br><i>*ARC provided by publisher as an exchange for honest review*</i></span>

<div id="review_654836664" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/654836664" />
    <a title="The Devil&#39;s Advocate" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20245504-the-devil-s-advocate"><img alt="The Devil&#39;s Advocate" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377517913p2/20245504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/654836664?book_show_action=true">Jun 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The Devil&#39;s Advocate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="The Devil&#39;s Advocate" href="/user/show/20245504-the-devil-s-advocate">The Devil&#39;s Advocate</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781456527730" href="/book/show/13111733-sempre">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE! </span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to The Devil's Advocate by: </span>
      Kristalia (◡‿◡✿) ♥Dex' &amp; Matt's Lady♥(◕‿◕✿) 
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20245504-the-devil-s-advocate?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20245504-the-devil-s-advocate?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer654836664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11196487604275096280"><br/><br/><a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/1044942_677989478894730_418748532_n_zpsa3610046.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427328i/854220.jpg' alt=' photo 1044942_677989478894730_418748532_n_zpsa3610046.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Dear Reader,<br/><br/><i>Sempre</i> is <b>not</b> your typical romance book. <br/><br/><b>Why?</b><br/><br/>Because the author managed to tug at the strings of my heart before I even started reading the story. <br/><br/><b>How?</b><br/><br/>Simply because of a mere introduction. This is how J.M. Darhower started her novel:<br/><br/><i>While <b>Sempre</b> is a work of fiction, the concept of modern-day slavery is not make-believe. There are an estimated 27 million people in the world today, coerced and forced into sexual or labor slavery. The majority of them are females, half being young</i></span>
  <span id="freeText11196487604275096280" style="display:none"><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/1044942_677989478894730_418748532_n_zpsa3610046.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427328i/854220.jpg" alt=" photo 1044942_677989478894730_418748532_n_zpsa3610046.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Dear Reader,<br><br><i>Sempre</i> is <b>not</b> your typical romance book. <br><br><b>Why?</b><br><br>Because the author managed to tug at the strings of my heart before I even started reading the story. <br><br><b>How?</b><br><br>Simply because of a mere introduction. This is how J.M. Darhower started her novel:<br><br><i>While <b>Sempre</b> is a work of fiction, the concept of modern-day slavery is not make-believe. There are an estimated 27 million people in the world today, coerced and forced into sexual or labor slavery. The majority of them are females, half being young girls. They’re our mothers, our fathers, our sisters, our brothers. They’re our friends, our lovers, our neighbors, our kids. They’re us. It could happen to anyone, even you.<br>Human trafficking is the second most lucrative crime in the world, making more money every year than Google, Nike, and Starbucks combined. It happens everywhere, from the poverty-stricken providences of Cambodia to the affluent suburbs of California. Two children are trafficked every minute-that’s a 2880 a day.<br>Become an abolitionist.<br>If we don’t fight for them, who will?</i><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/cm-51892-1512c5918e9370_zps255e2b7e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427328ra/854221.gif" alt=" photo cm-51892-1512c5918e9370_zps255e2b7e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was rendered speechless by those simple words. I started thinking about those people out there held against their will. I sympathized with them, and I cried for them. All of that was before I even started reading the story.<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/Jamie_zps44f544c5.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427328i/854222.png" alt=" photo Jamie_zps44f544c5.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Haven Antonelli, a second generation slave, grew up isolated in the middle of the desert, her days full of hard work and terrifying abuse. She never let herself hope for anything different in fear of constant disappointment. She knows that she will never be free.When Haven’s life is threatened, her mother orders her to run. And she does… But she soon finds herself in the hands of Dr. Vincent DeMarco, her new master…<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/boy-cute-guy-hot-man-Favimcom-111239_zpse775dfc1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427328i/854223.jpg" alt=" photo boy-cute-guy-hot-man-Favimcom-111239_zpse775dfc1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Carmine born into a wealthy Mafia family, lived a life of privilege, never having to answer for anything he did. He is the typical “bad boy”, rude, reckless, rash, and a trouble maker. Carmine is angry at the world…He is a broken soul, all vulnerable on the inside.<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/You-changed-my-life-without-even-trying_zpsfa5febdd2_zpsfc523f37.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427328i/854224.jpg" alt=" photo You-changed-my-life-without-even-trying_zpsfa5febdd2_zpsfc523f37.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But that changes when he meets Haven. <br><br>Carmine is immediately drawn to her fragility and innocence. However, his bad attitude scares her off, especially because he is her master’s son.<br><br>Entangled in a web of secrets and lies, they learn that while different on the surface, they have more in common than anyone would think.<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/you-made-me-complete-love-quote-timeline-profile-covers_zps372dea21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427328i/854225._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo you-made-me-complete-love-quote-timeline-profile-covers_zps372dea21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As months pass, Carmine and Haven fall in love…they start to heal each other slowly.<br><br><b>
  <i>“And I love you,” he said, his voice a whisper, but Haven felt it powerfully, deep down in her soul. “Ti amo, mia bella ragazza. Per sempre.”</i>
</b><br><br>What I loved about Carmine the most is that he had no problem apologizing for his faults. <br><br>The way he <b>showed</b> Haven his love, the way he tried to<b> understand</b> her, the way he wanted to <b>soothe</b> her pain, it gave romance a<b> new definition</b>.<br><br>I also loved the way he reassures Haven about his feelings for her. <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/tumblr_mosozd7Kkr1rcsm4to1_500_zpsae2f6aea.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427328ra/854226.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mosozd7Kkr1rcsm4to1_500_zpsae2f6aea.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As their love blossoms, Haven starts to hope again, live the life that should’ve been hers, and breathe freely. <br><br>Because for once, life is<i> GREEN</i>…<br> <br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/tumblr_m9zw0quqgj1rw8rduo1_500_zpsc090dfae.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427328ra/854227.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m9zw0quqgj1rw8rduo1_500_zpsc090dfae.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is not only a romantic, riveting, and exhilarating story about <b>hope</b>, <b>redemption</b>, <b>life</b>, <b>death</b>, and <b>love</b>.<br><br><i>Sempre</i> is about <b>surviving</b> in the most severe situations. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Life’s a struggle, and it would be so easy if it came with an eraser, but it didn’t. What’s done is done, as hard as that was to accept.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/devviereads/media/tumblr_m5fpowAz2q1r6mpdgo1_400_zpsc984388a1_zps2daa882b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427328ra/854228.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m5fpowAz2q1r6mpdgo1_400_zpsc984388a1_zps2daa882b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“One of the strangest things about living in the world is that only now and then one is quite sure one is going to live forever and ever and ever… sometimes a sound far-off music makes it true; and sometimes a look in some one’s eyes.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656611829" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here to read my review of the second book :)</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11196487604275096280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_308781822" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/308781822" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/308781822?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781456527730" href="/book/show/13111733-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=human-trafficking-slavery">human-trafficking-slavery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shy-heroine">shy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308781822" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10720405514025078009">Wow! This is astonishingly good book. If I could have given it more than 5 stars, I would have and I don’t even know if there are words to review it but I’m going to give it a go.<br/><br/>This is the story of Haven and Carmine. Haven is a slave born to a slave who was fathered by her master. She has known a life of intolerable cruelty, abuse, neglect and slavery. She is bought by Vincent DeMarco, a Mafioso, and taken to live with him and his 2 sons Carmine and Dominc. Dominic is a happy go lucky easy goi</span>
  <span id="freeText10720405514025078009" style="display:none">Wow! This is astonishingly good book. If I could have given it more than 5 stars, I would have and I don’t even know if there are words to review it but I’m going to give it a go.<br /><br />This is the story of Haven and Carmine. Haven is a slave born to a slave who was fathered by her master. She has known a life of intolerable cruelty, abuse, neglect and slavery. She is bought by Vincent DeMarco, a Mafioso, and taken to live with him and his 2 sons Carmine and Dominc. Dominic is a happy go lucky easy going teen but Carmine is the archetypal bad boy – a rebel without a cause. He’s seriously traumatised by witnessing his Mother’s murder as a child and is dark, unco-operative and antagonistic. He’s vain, selfish and arrogant and wears this as a suit of armour to prevent people from seeing the hurt deep inside and to close himself off from everyone emotionally.<br /><br />Haven starts her life at the De Marco’s battered, bruised, malnourished and underweight. She is terrified of putting a foot wrong and the ensuing punishment but she realises her life is better here and yet she is not free. She’s an amazingly drawn character – there’s a wide eyed innocence and awe to her which showed in the scene where she sat captivated by the fireflies caught in a jar. She’s amazed and captivated by all the new things in her life but she’s also a victim of her experiences and is cautious and terrified and wordly beyond her years in that respect. There’s an inner strength to her – she may not be free but her mind soars and there’s an integrity to her that allows her to see beyond Carmine’s armour to the person he should always have been.<br /><br />Carmine, when he finally takes notice of her, is so taken by her. He’s had a succession of girls for sex, never allowing them to get close or kiss them on the lips – he’s a real manwhore at school. He sees something in Haven, something which helps him rediscover the part of him he thought had died with his mother. She moves him, makes him fiercely protective and possessive and allows him to become the person he should have been. He’s horrified by her past experiences and wants, more than anything, for Haven to be free.<br /><br />They fall in love slowly and plenty of time is given to telling this part of the story and it is simply beautiful. I was tearing up on more than one occasion and the emotions, so beautifully expressed, hit me right in the solar plexus, it’s just soul deep. Their first kiss is just stunning. More than anything, Carmine wants Haven to be free but he’s just a kid but knows he is growing up in the Cosa Nostra and will one day achieve this goal for her.<br /><br />Just as their love is deepening into something very permanent, events set in motion before Haven was even born, start to surface and all hell is unleashed around them and, without giving away too much, Carmine has to make a huge sacrifice to free Haven and that’s ultimately what this novel is about – sacrifice. Many people sacrifice their lives, their freedom and their choice in this one and it is all done in the name of love and loss and it is so very, very beautiful and heart wrenching.<br /><br />Carmine is an amazing character – he evolves from a vain and spoilt selfish teen through his love for Haven into a man who is willing to make the ultimate sacrifice for her. Haven would also make the same sacrifice for him. I see plenty of potential for a sequel here – much is left unresolved, threads unsecured at the end and I really don’t want to let them go. I want to see where Carmine’s decisions will take them now that Haven is free and there are still secrets being kept that could drastically change their direction. So come on JM Darhower – a sequel, if you please.<br /><br />The narrative in this one is beautiful and sighworthy and here’s a few that took my breath away.<br /><br /><i>“How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.”<br />“I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.”<br />“Why?”<br />“Because it doesn’t.” </i><br /><br /><br /><i>“I ran, too, you know. My mama told me to run away and leave her there. I only did it because she asked me to.”<br />“So you know the guilt I feel.”<br />She nodded. “But you didn’t let her down, Carmine. You did what she needed you to do.”<br />Carmine brushed away her tears. “And what’s that?”<br />“You survived.”<br /></i><br /><br /><br /><i>“Haven, I could never love someone like you, because there isn’t anyone like you,” he said. “You’re one of a kind.”<br /></i><br /><br /><br /><i>He ran the back of his fingers along her flushed cheek. His touch was soft, and she leaned her head in his direction. “My beautiful girl,” he said.<br />She took in his expression. “You think I’m beautiful?”<br />“I don’t think you’re beautiful, Haven,” he said. “I know you are.”<br /></i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10720405514025078009" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1710829310" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1710829310" />
    <a title="Grecia Robles" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43801560-grecia-robles"><img alt="Grecia Robles" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578037155p2/43801560.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1710829310?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grecia Robles" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grecia Robles" href="/user/show/43801560-grecia-robles">Grecia Robles</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=favoritos">favoritos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=virgin-heroine">virgin-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1710829310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6956529379950976731"><i><b>*** 5 Colpo di Fulmine STARS***</b> </i><br/><br/>Primeramente quiero agradecer a <b>AleJandra </b>, ya que sin ella no hubiera podido leer este maravilloso libro. Thank you so much eres un sol.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>She stroked her thumb across his cheek, sending tingling through him. “Do you really feel that?” “Yeah. It’s like you have static under your skin.” She smiled. “What do you think it is?” “Colpo di fulmine?” he suggested. She just stared at him, and he smiled. “I guess you’re gonna want a translation.” “Please.” “It’s when</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText6956529379950976731" style="display:none"><i><b>*** 5 Colpo di Fulmine STARS***</b> </i><br><br>Primeramente quiero agradecer a <b>AleJandra </b>, ya que sin ella no hubiera podido leer este maravilloso libro. Thank you so much eres un sol.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>She stroked her thumb across his cheek, sending tingling through him. “Do you really feel that?” “Yeah. It’s like you have static under your skin.” She smiled. “What do you think it is?” “Colpo di fulmine?” he suggested. She just stared at him, and he smiled. “I guess you’re gonna want a translation.” “Please.” “It’s when you’re drawn to someone so forcefully that it’s like being struck by lightning</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>Este libro es HERMOSO ES MAGIA PURA</b> y Goodreads debería de darle estrellas infinitas porque se lo merece.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475802252ra/20767809.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Desde la primera página que leí me enganchó, es un libro un poco largo, pero que no contiene relleno ni un capítulo o página está demás. Está narrado en tercera persona, a mí a veces no me gusta pero aquí me pareció perfecto porque sabías lo que pasaba con la mente de cada personaje. Es un libro tierno, tiene partes muy divertidas que me hicieron reír mucho, es tan romántico que derrama miel y tiene su parte de acción y como todo libro de mafia está lleno de secretos.<br><br><b>Me enamoré de este libro de cada palabra y frase escrita que contiene. </b><br>Narra la historia de dos adolescentes una esclava y un chico hijo de uno de los miembros de una familia italiana que pertenece a la cosa nostra, o sea un príncipe de la mafia; al principio parecen tan diferentes porque <b>¿Qué pueden tener en común una chica que es esclava y un chico rico? </b>pero por dentro son tan iguales ya que los dos están dañados llenos de cicatrices y quieren ser libres de la vida que les tocó <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1537694285ra/26341290.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Haven</u>
</b> es un personaje tan bonito, es inocente y muy dulce, vivió toda su vida siendo esclava y cuando por fin vió el mundo por primera vez, lo veía con tanto asombro y eso me hizo reflexionar que somos tan insensibles y damos todo por sentado que ya casi nada nos asombra por eso bien dicen que tenemos que ver la vida con ojos de niños. <br>Me encantó como fue evolucionando su personaje de ser una niña insegura y asustadiza a convertirse en alguien fuerte que toma sus propias decisiones.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>He might've taken my life, but he didn't break my spirit. No one did, and no one ever will. Don't let them break you. Don’t let them win. You fight the fight. It’s the only way to be free.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Carmine</u>
</b><i>Il mio bel ragazzo ti amo sei il mio colpo di fulmine</i><br>Caí enamorada desde que apareció, tengo una debilidad por los bad boys que por dentro son unos teddy bears, él es tan tan lindo es todo sarcástico no tiene filtro siempre dice lo que piensa, es finicky, picky malhablado y OMG ! cuando hablaba en italiano me derretía toda por dentro. <br><b>Carmine es TAN BELLO!! Aparentemente es todo brabucón, un bocazas a veces anda enojado explosivo pero en el fondo es todo lindo, es un alma bella y sensible. Es mi bebé hermoso y LO AMO!!</b><br>Mi personaje favorito <i>Per sempre</i>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1537694285ra/26341291.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No puedo explicar los sentimientos que me provocó el romance de Haven y Carmine, son de esos amores tan épicos que son insuperables y difícil de olvidar.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I love you,” he said, his voice a whisper, but Haven felt it powerfully, deep down in her soul. “Ti amo, mia bella ragazza. Per sempre.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Los personajes secundarios me encantaron empezando por Vicent y Corrado que los pasas de odiar a amar en un segundo y quiero deseo que tengan su HEA.<br><br>En conclusión este libro es fantástico y como ya saben me encantó, la temática de la mafia italiana me pareció tan increíble, ya que a pesar de que hacen cosas ilegales tienen ese código de honorabilidad la famiglia está primero y me hizo tener esa doble moral porque quiero que los corruptos y delincuentes paguen pero aquí los defendía.<br><br><b>1 Rereading Sep 2017</b><br><b> 2 Rereading Sep 2018</b><br><b> 3 Rereading Sep 2019</b><br><br>Cada vez que leo este libro me gusta más y lo sufro más .<br>Carmine sigue siendo mi bebé Hermoso malhablado, picky con el alma buena y Haven siguen siendo esa niña dulce, ingenua que ve la vida por primera vez y que ama con todo su corazón a Carmine.<br><br>Pero el que cada vez que leo esta historia me gusta más y es Vincent De Marco, su historia de amor me parte el alma, cada vez que leo como sufre Vincent me desgarra el corazón y es que la primera vez que leí el libro empecé odiándolo pero ahora ya es la tercera vez, el segundo libro lo he leído dos veces y leí made la precuela entonces ya la veo con otros ojos ya lo entiendo y quisiera tener el poder de quitarle todo su sufrimiento, como quisiera que las cosas hubieran sido diferentes para él. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462463287ra/19000947.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Una tercera lectura que disfruté de principio a fin, terminé amando el libro más si es que se puede.<br><br>BTW… No había caído en cuenta con el personaje de Natalia ni en la primera ni en la segunda lectura pero después de lo que me enteré en Made OMG!!! La autora nos dejó inconcluso ese asunto.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6956529379950976731" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_503873535" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503873535" />
    <a title="K" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16359109-k"><img alt="K" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357989852p2/16359109.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503873535?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/16359109-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781456527730" href="/book/show/13111733-sempre">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=tattooed-pierced-hero">tattooed-pierced-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=messed-up-hero">messed-up-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=arrogant-hero">arrogant-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=hero-alpha-obsessed-jealous">hero-alpha-obsessed-jealous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=heart-wrenching">heart-wrenching</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503873535" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5351381611723081491"><b>5+ PERFECT STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384902050i/7023273.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"―Hummingbird?―Yeah, hummingbird. Colibri. You kinda remind me of one. ―Why? ―I don‘t know. They‘re these little birds that flutter around and hum. And you know, you‘re kinda the same way."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This book was absolutely amazing!<i>Sempre,</i> can almost be interpreted as a messed up version of Cinderella..if Cinderella was in the mafia business. We have the mistreated female servant who falls in love with the wealthy and very handsome prince.. except in this story the prince is</span>
  <span id="freeText5351381611723081491" style="display:none"><b>5+ PERFECT STARS!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384902050i/7023273.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"―Hummingbird?―Yeah, hummingbird. Colibri. You kinda remind me of one. ―Why? ―I don‘t know. They‘re these little birds that flutter around and hum. And you know, you‘re kinda the same way."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book was absolutely amazing!<i>Sempre,</i> can almost be interpreted as a messed up version of Cinderella..if Cinderella was in the mafia business. We have the mistreated female servant who falls in love with the wealthy and very handsome prince.. except in this story the prince is dropping the f#$%! bomb every 3 sentences. Darhower does an amazing job of making you <b>fall just as in love with this story as the ever classic, Cinderella. *sigh*</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Ti amo, mia bella ragazza. Per sempre." "Sempre?" She asked. Cracking a smile, he brushed his finger softly across her lips. "Always and forever"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>CARMEN FREAKING DEMARCO</b> will you <i>please marry me right now?</i> Like right now! I have to have you for myself. <b>Carmen is one of my all time favorite book boyfriends.</b> He's jsut one of those love able bad boys that we can't resist!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387351657i/7582448.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Grabbing her hand, he pressed it gently to his chest. His skin was warm to the touch, and she could slightly feel his pulse pounding against her palm. “Do you feel that? I’m not going anywhere, Haven. This is yours."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>At over 500+ pages, I thought for sure this book would lose my attention but it never did. It was <b>consistently captivating from start to finish.</b> The characters were so fantastically well written that you fall in love with all of them. Carmine &amp; Haven grew and matured over the book, and I fell in love with the supporting cast as well.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"They were two broken kids, desperate to be whole again, struggling to find balance in a world out of their control."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Sempre is now officially going to be classified as one of my all-time favorites.</b> Besides the heartbreaking realization of Haven's slavery filled world and the disheartening circumstances that surrounded Carmine &amp; Haven's love for one another, there was also a comedic feel to this book that kept it from becoming too dark or disturbing. Seriously, Darhower is a freaking genius and I can't wait for book 2.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Despite everything, he was still her world, her one and only. Part of her may have felt dead, but there was still another part of her that lived for Carmine DeMarco."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book had it all, an epic love that made my heart clench; sadness and gut wrenching moments that will make you cry. The entire time I was reading this I was nervous for I knew that something horrible was just going to happen...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Carmine‘s heart felt like it was being ripped apart, his voice an agonized whisper. ―Why did they have to take my hummingbird?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>If you are considering reading this you absolutely should. This book has something in it for everyone. <b>Seriously, go pick it up right now. Right now.</b> It sat on my TBR list forever.. and I hate hate hate that I missed out and waited so long to read it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387351499i/7582439.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“How about we just be Haven and Carmine?” she suggested. “We don’t know the ending, but we can always hope for the best.” “I like that,” he said. “Besides, there’s a reason we don’t know how the story ends.” “Why?” “Because it doesn't.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=usdIB4aU1fQ" rel="nofollow noopener">LISTEN TO THE SONG THAT CARMINE SINGS TO HAVEN!</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5351381611723081491" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2035905354" />
    <a title="Svetlana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68791366-svetlana"><img alt="Svetlana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511141526p2/68791366.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2035905354?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Svetlana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Svetlana" href="/user/show/68791366-svetlana">Svetlana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68791366-svetlana?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68791366-svetlana?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68791366-svetlana?shelf=completed-series">completed-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2035905354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1104796305444564288">You know, I actually really enjoyed this book. I was so hesitant to pick it up at first because I didn't know if I was going to like it. But I'm so glad I gave it a read wooot wooot! The story started off a bit slow and it took me a while to warm up and connect to the characters. But once I was in.. BAM! I was IN! <i>
  <b>Angst</b>
</i> should be Darhower's other name because damn. The sis really knows how to write a book which oozes it. <br/><br/>The story hugely dealt with Mafia organisations and how it impacted tho</span>
  <span id="freeText1104796305444564288" style="display:none">You know, I actually really enjoyed this book. I was so hesitant to pick it up at first because I didn't know if I was going to like it. But I'm so glad I gave it a read wooot wooot! The story started off a bit slow and it took me a while to warm up and connect to the characters. But once I was in.. BAM! I was IN! <i>
  <b>Angst</b>
</i> should be Darhower's other name because damn. The sis really knows how to write a book which oozes it. <br /><br />The story hugely dealt with Mafia organisations and how it impacted those who were a part of it. Everyone just whipped out their guns and went <i>
  <b>PEW PEW PEW</b>
</i> at every little thing. You'd get a bullet between your eyes for simply looking the wrong way. But my favourite part of the story were the characters. They all had such messy and unpredictable lives due their associations with <i>
  <b>la famiglia</b>
</i>. Yet they were incredibly passionate people. They'd sacrifice themselves for those they loved and they hated with the same intensity. <br /><br />I know this isn't everyone's thang but if it is yours then definitely check it out!</span>

<div id="review_1643492907" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1643492907" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1643492907?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beatrice by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/21106490-camille-santos">Camille Santos</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1643492907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9545686536814622823">Many thanks to my book girlfriend, Camille, for recommending this book to me. <3 This book has been on my TBR for ages and I finally get to pick this book up. Just the perfect timing I'm still on the mood for Mafia/Assassin themed books (currently obsessing with it).<br/><br/><b>Haven Antonelli</b> grew up as a slave with her mother and they're both abused for years. She lived her whole life being afraid because of it and never lose hope that one day, she'll be free. When <b>Dr. Vincent DeMarco</b>-- a Mafia member-- t</span>
  <span id="freeText9545686536814622823" style="display:none">Many thanks to my book girlfriend, Camille, for recommending this book to me. &lt;3 This book has been on my TBR for ages and I finally get to pick this book up. Just the perfect timing I'm still on the mood for Mafia/Assassin themed books (currently obsessing with it).<br /><br /><b>Haven Antonelli</b> grew up as a slave with her mother and they're both abused for years. She lived her whole life being afraid because of it and never lose hope that one day, she'll be free. When <b>Dr. Vincent DeMarco</b>-- a Mafia member-- took her, she's adjusting to a new rich life that she never had. She still works hard for doing household chores and has yet to earn Dr. DeMarco's trust. Also she met his sons, Dominic DeMarco and <b>Carmine DeMarco</b>. Carmine somewhat made her curious. He has this bad boy image and he has a strained relationship with his father because of what happened in the past. They're both longing for someone and understand each other's feelings despite of being flawed. So many things happened and everything has put them into a test. <br /><br /><i>Sempre</i> is simply a gem and it gave me a bad case of book hangover. It took me a while to write something and organize my thoughts. Oh my god. <b>What a beautiful story between a slave and a mafia prince (a hot-damn-<i>colpo di fulmine</i>-worthy- mafia - prince) </b>. I think this is a perfect book to start when you're going to dive in to Mafia themed books for the following reasons:<br /><br />- It's somewhat in between YA and NA.<br />- <b>Trigger warning:</b> there is an abuse but it's less graphic/violent. Not to the point you will cringe. I find it mild unlike the other ones I've read.<br />- It focuses more on the character / family drama. <br /><br />The plot is well written and each scenes are very detailed. J.M Darhower's writing style is hands down beautiful and I'm fully engrossed with the story. The romance between the characters is absolutely <b>slow burn</b> and the other thing that I love about this entire novel, <b>all the characters aren't left out</b>. Everyone has their role in the story and they played it so good and they're all complex. <b>Dr. DeMarco is probably the most complex character.</b> He's a broken and stern man with a huge heart. Carmine may not understand his good intentions, but I love how he's protective of him and doesn't want his son to expose into a dangerous life. He wants Carmine to live free and not follow his footsteps. Whatever happens, he's there for his son for good and bad times. <br /><br />Haven is indeed a strong heroine. She's selfless, loving and caring. Her character development is such a wonderful thing to see.Grab me some cherry coke and let me fangirl on <b>Carmine DeMarco</b>. My Mafia Prince. Goodness lord, I'm a sucker for bad boys. He's a sweet bad boy and his love for Haven... <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>"Haven, I could never love someone like you, because there isn't anyone else like you. You're one of a kind."</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />eeeeeee!!! *squeals more like a banshee*I swear there are more swoon worthy quotes, especially what <i>Colpo di fulmine</i> means (not going to mention it here because you need to find out) and Overall, I love this book..<i>per sempre</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9545686536814622823" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1095134325" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1095134325" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1095134325?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-dark-contemporary">new-adult-dark-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=november-reads">november-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1095134325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13014508270099657852">What an amazing story! I thoroughly enjoyed this mafia romance; and the love that develops between Carmine and Haven is truly EPIC! We have two teenagers who are far totally different walks of life. Carmine is basically considered a "Mafia Prince" (even though his father is fighting for his son not to be involved in "the life"); and then we have Haven who was saved by Vincent (Carmine's father)from a life of slavery. Although, to Haven it feels like she has moved from one Master's house to anoth</span>
  <span id="freeText13014508270099657852" style="display:none">What an amazing story! I thoroughly enjoyed this mafia romance; and the love that develops between Carmine and Haven is truly EPIC! We have two teenagers who are far totally different walks of life. Carmine is basically considered a "Mafia Prince" (even though his father is fighting for his son not to be involved in "the life"); and then we have Haven who was saved by Vincent (Carmine's father)from a life of slavery. Although, to Haven it feels like she has moved from one Master's house to another. She trusts no one, and I can't say I blame her. As time goes on though she gets to know the sons of Vincent..and I must say that I was impressed with both of them. Dominic is the oldest one, but he has a heart of gold-he really does. I am amazed the lengths that he goes to make Haven feel comforted, accepted, and never less than himself. Carmine is a tougher guy to like at first. He disrespects the girls that he is "sleeping with," he has extreme anger issues...Oh let's face it..he has so many issues it is hard to keep up. Not many truly like him, because he is just a plain a-hole that has no regard for anyone including himself and his own well being. Then along comes Haven, and these two bring out the best in each other. Carmine does a total personality change, and amazingly as he falls in love with Haven he is as loyal as they come. I fell in love with him; but also with Haven too. They belonged together, and if I have ever doubted fate in my romance books, this is the book that makes me a firm believer in it! <br /><br />There is so much that takes place in this story, it has it all: drama,betrayal,humor,love,grief...you name it; it has it. I loved the journey that the author takes us on, and it is one of those books that I became fully absorbed into the lives of the characters. The past few days I have been walking around in a daze, as even when I closed the book; it was still playing in my mind! To me, that is the definition of an Epic book, and a brilliant author. Sempre goes on my keeper shelf for sure, and I can even see that down the road I would be interested in rereading it again! I won't ever forget the lengths that Carmine goes through for the love of his life. He is so dedicated to Haven, and just thinking about it melts me.<br /><br />Do I highly recommend this book...Absolutely, I do! I am kicking myself that I waited to read it for so long! Just a top quality book that I will never forget. Sempre will go down as one of my all time best romance books! Thank you J.M. Darhower for delivering such a masterpiece!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13014508270099657852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review586584217">
  <td colspan="2">
